And looks like we'll be back at window two for this as well. This is Artemis Mission Control. About seven minutes ago, the Orion spacecraft executed the outbound trajectory correction three burn to fine-tune the trajectory of the Orion spacecraft as it continues to make its way around the moon with that lunar flyby planned for tomorrow on flight day six. Now that that outbound trajectory correction burn is complete, teams will be maneuvering the Orion spacecraft into an attitude to be able to capture some opportunistic imaging of the moon.
